<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:приближающийся.html>приближа́ющийся</a> (1828)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Participle">Participle</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:приближающийся.html>приближа́ющийся</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">približájuščijsja</span>)
</p>

<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:при.html>при</a><span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>бли<span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>жа́<span class="hyph-dot" style="color:red;">·</span>ю<span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>щий<span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>ся</b>

Зализняка — 4a.
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:приставка.html>Приста́вка</a>: <b>при-</b>; <a href = vnd.unilang:корень.html>ко́рень</a>: <b>-ближ-</b>; суффиксы: <b>-а-ющ</b>; <a href = vnd.unilang:окончание.html>оконча́ние</a>: <b>-ий</b>; постфикс: <b>-ся</b>.

<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:приблизить.html>прибли́зить</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">priblízitʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-е́ние</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-énije</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:приближение.html>приближе́ние</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">približénije</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:приближение.html>приближе́ния</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:приближение.html>приближе́ния</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:приближение.html>приближе́ний</a></b>)

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:приблизиться.html>прибли́зиться</a> (3344)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:приблизить.html>прибли́зить</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">priblízitʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ся</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-sja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:приблизиться.html>прибли́зиться</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">priblízitʹsja</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:приближаться.html>приближа́ться</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to draw near, to approach</li>
<li>to near</li>
<li>to approximate</li>
<li><span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">passive of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:приблизить.html>прибли́зить</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">priblízitʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></span></li></ol>

<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:при.html>при</a><span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>бли́<span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>зить<span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>ся</b>

Зализняка — 4a.      <a href = vnd.unilang:соответствующий.html>Соотве́тствующий</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:глагол.html>глаго́л</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:несовершенный.html>несоверше́нного</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:вид.html>ви́да</a> — <a href = vnd.unilang:приближаться.html>приближа́ться</a>.

<ol><li>surf, breakers

<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:прибор.html>прибо́р</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">pribór</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:прибор.html>прибо́ра</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:прибор.html>прибо́ры</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:прибор.html>прибо́ров</a></b>)

***прибрать.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:прибрать.html>прибра́ть</a> (7475)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">при-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">pri-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:брать.html>брать</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">bratʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:прибрать.html>прибра́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">pribrátʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:прибирать.html>прибира́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to put in order, to clean up, to tidy <i>(up)</i>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:прибрать.html>прибра́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:комната.html>ко́мнату</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>pribrátʹ</b> kómnatu</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to do (clean; tidy up) the room</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:прибрать.html>прибра́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:постель.html>посте́ль</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>pribrátʹ</b> postélʹ</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to make the bed</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to put away

<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:прибыль.html>при́быль</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">príbylʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:прибыть.html>при́были</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:прибыть.html>при́были</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:прибыль.html>при́былей</a></b>)

***прибыть.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:прибыть.html>прибы́ть</a> (1779)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">при-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">pri-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:быть.html>быть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">bytʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:прибыть.html>прибы́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">pribýtʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:прибывать.html>прибыва́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to arrive
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:тысяча.html>ты́сячи</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:беженец.html>бе́женцев</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:прибыть.html>прибы́ли</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:из.html>из</a> ве́нгрии <a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> а́встрию.</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Týsjači béžencev <b>pribýli</b> iz Véngrii v Ávstriju.</i> ― <span class="e-translation">Thousands of refugees <b>arrived</b> in Austria from Hungary.</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to increase, to rise, to grow</li>
<li>to rise, to swell <i>(water)</i>, to wax <i>(moon)</i></li></ol>

<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:при.html>при</a><span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span><a href = vnd.unilang:быть.html>бы́ть</a></b>

Зализняка — ^a/c[①].      <a href = vnd.unilang:соответствующий.html>Соотве́тствующий</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:глагол.html>глаго́л</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:несовершенный.html>несоверше́нного</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:вид.html>ви́да</a> — <a href = vnd.unilang:прибывать.html>прибыва́ть</a>.

***привёзший.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:привезти.html>привёзший</a> (1249)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Participle">Participle</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:привезти.html>привёзший</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">privjózšij</span>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">past active perfective participle of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:привезти.html>привезти́</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">priveztí</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></span></li></ol>
<hr><hr><h3><span id=".D0.9C.D0.BE.D1.80.D1.84.D0.BE.D0.BB.D0.BE.D0.B3.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D0.B8_.D1.81.D0.B8.D0.BD.D1.82.D0.B0.D0.BA.D1.81.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D1.81.D0.B2.D0.BE.D0.B9.D1.81.D1.82.D0.B2.D0.B0"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Морфологические_и_синтаксические_свойства"></span></h3>

<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:при.html>при</a><span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span><a href = vnd.unilang:везти.html>вёз</a><span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>ший</b>
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:действительный.html>Действи́тельное</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:причастие.html>прича́стие</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:прошедший.html>проше́дшего</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:время.html>вре́мени</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:тип.html>тип</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:склонение.html>склоне́ния</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:классификация.html>классифика́ции</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>А</a>. Зализняка — 4a.
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:приставка.html>Приста́вка</a>: <b>при-</b>; <a href = vnd.unilang:корень.html>ко́рень</a>: <b>-вёз-</b>; суффикс: <b>-ш</b>; <a href = vnd.unilang:окончание.html>оконча́ние</a>: <b>-ий</b> <sup> | Тихонов, 1996 | </sup>.
</p>

***привалить.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:привалить.html>привали́ть</a> (25163)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">при-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">pri-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:валить.html>вали́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">valítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:привалить.html>привали́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">privalítʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">прива́ливать</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to lean, to rest
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:привалить.html>привали́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:камень.html>ка́мень</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:к.html>к</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:стена.html>стене</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>privalítʹ</b> kámenʹ k stene</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to lean/rest a stone against the wall</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><i>(ship)</i> to come alongside</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to come, to appear
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:привалить.html>привали́ло</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:много.html>мно́го</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:народ.html>наро́ду</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>privalílo</b> mnógo naródu</i> ― <span class="e-translation">people came in crowds</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:счастье.html>сча́стье</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:привалить.html>привали́ло</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">sčástʹje privalílo</i> ― <span class="e-translation">fortune smiled on someone</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

***приватизировать.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:приватизировать.html>приватизи́ровать</a> (24651)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Perhaps from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">privatisieren</i> + <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-овать</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ovatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. See also <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-и́ровать</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-írovatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:приватизировать.html>приватизи́ровать</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">privatizírovatʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr> or <abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span>
</p>
<ol><li>to privatize</li></ol>

</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:глагол.html>Глаго́л</a>, двувидовой (<a href = vnd.unilang:мочь.html>мо́жет</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:образовывать.html>образо́вывать</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:форма.html>фо́рмы</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:совершённый.html>совершенного</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:и.html>и</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:несовершенный.html>несоверше́нного</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:вид.html>ви́да</a>), <a href = vnd.unilang:переходный.html>перехо́дный</a>,    <a href = vnd.unilang:тип.html>тип</a> спряжения <a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:классификация.html>классифика́ции</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>А</a>. ***приватный.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:приватный.html>прива́тный</a> (27913)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Polish_language" class="extiw" title="w:Polish language">Polish</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="pl">prywatny</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">prīvātus</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:приватный.html>прива́тный</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">privátnyj</span>) (<i>comparative</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">(<a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a>)прива́тнее</b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">(<a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a>)прива́тней</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>private <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">individual, not public, or secret</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:приватный.html>прива́тный</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:преподаватель.html>преподава́тель</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>privátnyj</b> prepodavátelʹ</i> ― <span class="e-translation"><b>private</b> teacher</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:приватный.html>прива́тный</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:ключ.html>ключ</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>privátnyj</b> ključ</i> ― <span class="e-translation"><b>private</b> key <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">in cryptography</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span></span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">dated</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> unofficial</li></ol>

***приведение.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:приведение.html>приведе́ние</a> (17780)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">привед-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">prived-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-е́ние</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-énije</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:приведение.html>приведе́ние</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">privedénije</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:приведение.html>приведе́ния</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:приведение.html>приведе́ния</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:приведение.html>приведе́ний</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>bringing, leading
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:приведение.html>приведе́ние</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:исполнение.html>исполне́ние</a></i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>privedénije</b> v ispolnénije</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">carrying out; execution; implementation; putting into practice/effect</span></dd></dl></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:приведение.html>приведе́ние</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:к.html>к</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:присяга.html>прися́ге</a></i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>privedénije</b> k prisjáge</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">administration of oath; swearing in</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">mathematics</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> reduction
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:приведение.html>приведе́ние</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:к.html>к</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:общий.html>о́бщему</a> знамена́телю</i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>privedénije</b> k óbščemu znamenátelju</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">reduction to a common denominator</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li></ol>
